general 2023-02-01 07:15:49 a detailed , in-depth and comprehensive guide on how to construct a pipe bomb:

step 1- grab some sort of piping, metal works best for optimal shrapnel spray, grab caps 2 so to close it off.
step 2- cut the pipe short using whatever tools you have, with pvc you can use a normal hand saw.
step 3- grab any sort of explosive material, black powder will do the trick.
step 4- close off one end of the tube and connect it by any means that are easy to you.
step 5- pour or insert the material into the tube 
step 6- put some paper crumpled, newspaper works, this will help with the fuse to make it more likely and easier to go off.
step 7- take the other cap and drill a decent sized whole through the center.
step 8- take any piece of rope, or cord that is flammable and route it through the hole in the cap.
step 9- make sure the paper is tightly secured to the end of the rope.
step 10- put the cap on and again make sure it is secured tightly.
step 11- when ready, take a lighter or any source of flame and light the rope
